When\n * it encounters a newer version, it parses it using the current format. This basically means\n * that new versions cannot remove or reorder any of the existing fields.\n */\npublic class ConsumerProtocol {\n    public static final String PROTOCOL_TYPE = \"consumer\";\n\n    static {\n        // Safety check to ensure that both parts of the consumer protocol remain in sync.\n        if (ConsumerProtocolSubscription.LOWEST_SUPPORTED_VERSION\n                != ConsumerProtocolAssignment.LOWEST_SUPPORTED_VERSION)\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Subscription and Assignment schemas must have the \" +\n                \"same lowest version\");\n\n        if (ConsumerProtocolSubscription.HIGHEST_SUPPORTED_VERSION\n                != ConsumerProtocolAssignment.HIGHEST_SUPPORTED_VERSION)\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Subscription and Assignment schemas must have the \" +\n                \"same highest version\");\n    }\n\n    public static short deserializeVersion(final ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        try {\n            return buffer.getShort();\n        } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n            throw new SchemaException(\"Buffer underflow while parsing consumer protocol's header\", e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static ByteBuffer serializeSubscription(final Subscription subscription) {\n        return serializeSubscription(subscription, ConsumerProtocolSubscription.HIGHEST_SUPPORTED_VERSION);\n    }\n\n    public static ByteBuffer serializeSubscription(final Subscription subscription, short version) {\n        version = checkSubscriptionVersion(version);\n\n        ConsumerProtocolSubscription data = new ConsumerProtocolSubscription();\n\n        List<String> topics = new ArrayList<>(subscription.topics());\n        Collections.sort(topics);\n        data.setTopics(topics);\n\n        data.setUserData(subscription.userData() != null ? subscription.userData().duplicate() : null);\n\n        List<TopicPartition> ownedPartitions = new ArrayList<>(subscription.ownedPartitions());\n        ownedPartitions.sort(Comparator.comparing(TopicPartition::topic).thenComparing(TopicPartition::partition));\n        ConsumerProtocolSubscription.TopicPartition partition = null;\n        for (TopicPartition tp : ownedPartitions) {\n            if (partition == null || !partition.topic().equals(tp.topic())) {\n                partition = new ConsumerProtocolSubscription.TopicPartition().setTopic(tp.topic());\n                data.ownedPartitions().add(partition);\n            }\n            partition.partitions().add(tp.partition());\n        }\n        subscription.rackId().ifPresent(data::setRackId);\n\n        data.setGenerationId(subscription.generationId().orElse(-1));\n        return MessageUtil.toVersionPrefixedByteBuffer(version, data);\n    }\n\n    public static Subscription deserializeSubscription(final ByteBuffer buffer, short version) {\n        version = checkSubscriptionVersion(version);\n\n        try {\n            ConsumerProtocolSubscription data =\n                new ConsumerProtocolSubscription(new ByteBufferAccessor(buffer), version);\n\n            List<TopicPartition> ownedPartitions = new ArrayList<>();\n            for (ConsumerProtocolSubscription.TopicPartition tp : data.ownedPartitions()) {\n                for (Integer partition : tp.partitions()) {\n                    ownedPartitions.add(new TopicPartition(tp.topic(), partition));\n                }\n            }\n\n            return new Subscription(\n                data.topics(),\n                data.userData() != null ? data.userData().duplicate() : null,\n                ownedPartitions,\n                data.generationId(),\n                data.rackId() == null || data.rackId().isEmpty() ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(data.rackId()));\n        } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n            throw new SchemaException(\"Buffer underflow while parsing consumer protocol's subscription\", e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static Subscription deserializeSubscription(final ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return deserializeSubscription(buffer, deserializeVersion(buffer));\n    }\n\n    public static ConsumerProtocolSubscription deserializeConsumerProtocolSubscription(\n        final ByteBuffer buffer,\n        short version\n    ) {\n        version = checkSubscriptionVersion(version);\n\n        try {\n            return new ConsumerProtocolSubscription(new ByteBufferAccessor(buffer), version);\n        } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n            throw new SchemaException(\"Buffer underflow while parsing consumer protocol's subscription\", e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static ConsumerProtocolSubscription deserializeConsumerProtocolSubscription(\n        final ByteBuffer buffer\n    ) {\n        return deserializeConsumerProtocolSubscription(buffer, deserializeVersion(buffer));\n    }\n\n    public static ByteBuffer serializeAssignment(final Assignment assignment) {\n        return serializeAssignment(assignment, ConsumerProtocolAssignment.HIGHEST_SUPPORTED_VERSION);\n    }\n","numLines":150,"startLine":1,"totalLines":233}}}

The state machine defines three primary protocol phases: Join, Sync, and Rebalance.\\n\\n## State Machine Architecture\\n\\n### Core State Definitions\\n\\n**ClassicGroupState.java** defines the group-level state enum for the classic consumer group protocol with five states:\\n- EMPTY: Group has no members\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE: Join phase - members are joining and waiting\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Sync phase - members synchronizing assignments\\n- STABLE: Normal operation\\n- DEAD: Group being removed\\n\\nThe state machine also defines valid state transitions through the `validPreviousStates()` method, which enforces the protocol flow.\\n\\n**ConsumerGroup.java** implements the modern consumer group protocol (KIP-848) with a different state progression:\\n- EMPTY -> ASSIGNING -> RECONCILING -> STABLE\\nThese states more directly correspond to the join/sync phases.\\n\\n### State Transition Implementation\\n\\n**ClassicGroup.java** implements the `transitionTo()` method that performs state transitions with validation. The method calls `assertValidTransition()` to ensure only valid state transitions occur according to the state machine definition.\\n\\n### Join Phase Operations\\n\\n**GroupMetadataManager.java** implements the join phase through multiple methods:\\n- `classicGroupJoin()`: Public entry point for handling JoinGroup requests\\n- `classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup()`: Routes join requests to classic groups\\n- `classicGroupJoinNewMember()`: Handles new member joins\\n- `classicGroupJoinExistingMember()`: Handles existing member rejoin\\n- `classicGroupJoinNewStaticMember()` / `classicGroupJoinNewDynamicMember()`: Specific member type handling\\n- `maybeCompleteJoinPhase()`: Detects when all members have joined\\n- `completeClassicGroupJoin()`: Transitions from PREPARING_REBALANCE to COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n\\nDuring the join phase, the group state transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE where members wait for all expected members to join.\\n\\n### Sync Phase Operations\\n\\n**GroupMetadataManager.java** implements the sync phase through:\\n- `classicGroupSync()`: Public entry point for handling SyncGroup requests\\n- `schedulePendingSync()`: Schedules sync operations\\n- Sync operations transition the group from COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE\\n\\nThe sync phase waits for all members to submit their synchronized assignments before transitioning to STABLE state.\\n\\n### Rebalance Phase\\n\\nThe rebalance phase is triggered when:\\n- A member fails (detected via heartbeat timeout)\\n- A member leaves the group\\n- A member sends a new JoinGroup with updated metadata\\n- New members join during STABLE state\\n\\nThese events cause a transition back to PREPARING_REBALANCE, starting a new rebalance cycle.\\n\\n### Member State Management\\n\\n**MemberState.java** defines the member-level reconciliation states:\\n- STABLE: Member is fully reconciled\\n- UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS: Member must revoke some partitions\\n- UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS: Member waiting for partition releases\\n\\n### Support Classes\\n\\n**GroupCoordinatorService.java** and **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** orchestrate the state machine execution across the cluster.\\n\\n**CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java** implements the target assignment building and reconciliation state machine for partition assignment.\\n\\n**ClassicGroupMember.java** and **ConsumerGroupMember.java** track individual member state during protocol phases.\\n\\n## State Transition Flow\\n\\nThe complete state transition chain for a rebalance cycle:\\n\\n1. EMPTY/STABLE → PREPARING_REBALANCE (join phase triggered)\\n2. PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE (all members joined, ready for sync)\\n3. COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE (all members synced, rebalance complete)\\n4. ],\n  \"text\": \"The consumer group coordinator's state machine is implemented across multiple Java source files in the apache/kafka group-coordinator module. The state machine defines three primary protocol phases: Join, Sync, and Rebalance.\\n\\n## State Machine Architecture\\n\\n### Core State Definitions\\n\\n**ClassicGroupState.java** defines the group-level state enum for the classic consumer group protocol with five states:\\n- EMPTY: Group has no members\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE: Join phase - members are joining and waiting\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Sync phase - members synchronizing assignments\\n- STABLE: Normal operation\\n- DEAD: Group being removed\\n\\nThe state machine also defines valid state transitions through the `validPreviousStates()` method, which enforces the protocol flow.\\n\\n**ConsumerGroup.java** implements the modern consumer group protocol (KIP-848) with a different state progression:\\n- EMPTY -> ASSIGNING -> RECONCILING -> STABLE\\nThese states more directly correspond to the join/sync phases.\\n\\n### State Transition Implementation\\n\\n**ClassicGroup.java** implements the `transitionTo()` method that performs state transitions with validation. The method calls `assertValidTransition()` to ensure only valid state transitions occur according to the state machine definition.\\n\\n### Join Phase Operations\\n\\n**GroupMetadataManager.java** implements the join phase through multiple methods:\\n- `classicGroupJoin()`: Public entry point for handling JoinGroup requests\\n- `classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup()`: Routes join requests to classic groups\\n- `classicGroupJoinNewMember()`: Handles new member joins\\n- `classicGroupJoinExistingMember()`: Handles existing member rejoin\\n- `classicGroupJoinNewStaticMember()` / `classicGroupJoinNewDynamicMember()`: Specific member type handling\\n- `maybeCompleteJoinPhase()`: Detects when all members have joined\\n- `completeClassicGroupJoin()`: Transitions from PREPARING_REBALANCE to COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n\\nDuring the join phase, the group state transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE where members wait for all expected members to join.\\n\\n### Sync Phase Operations\\n\\n**GroupMetadataManager.java** implements the sync phase through:\\n- `classicGroupSync()`: Public entry point for handling SyncGroup requests\\n- `schedulePendingSync()`: Schedules sync operations\\n- Sync operations transition the group from COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE\\n\\nThe sync phase waits for all members to submit their synchronized assignments before transitioning to STABLE state.\\n\\n### Rebalance Phase\\n\\nThe rebalance phase is triggered when:\\n- A member fails (detected via heartbeat timeout)\\n- A member leaves the group\\n- A member sends a new JoinGroup with updated metadata\\n- New members join during STABLE state\\n\\nThese events cause a transition back to PREPARING_REBALANCE, starting a new rebalance cycle.\\n\\n### Member State Management\\n\\n**MemberState.java** defines the member-level reconciliation states:\\n- STABLE: Member is fully reconciled\\n- UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS: Member must revoke some partitions\\n- UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS: Member waiting for partition releases\\n\\n### Support Classes\\n\\n**GroupCoordinatorService.java** and **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** orchestrate the state machine execution across the cluster.\\n\\n**CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java** implements the target assignment building and reconciliation state machine for partition assignment.\\n\\n**ClassicGroupMember.java** and **ConsumerGroupMember.java** track individual member state during protocol phases.\\n\\n## State Transition Flow\\n\\nThe complete state transition chain for a rebalance cycle:\\n\\n1. EMPTY/STABLE → PREPARING_REBALANCE (join phase triggered)\\n2. PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE (all members joined, ready for sync)\\n3. COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE (all members synced, rebalance complete)\\n4. STABLE → PREPARING_REBALANCE (rebalance triggered by event)\\n\\nThese transitions are validated through the ClassicGroupState's state machine definition, ensuring that invalid state transitions cannot occur.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
